<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;99.1</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="704" height="108" src="g90281mai001.jpg"></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE
RELEASE</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">McCORMICK REPORTS RECORD RESULTS FOR
FIRST QUARTER OF 2008</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Sales increased 11%.&#160; Consumer business sales rose 10% and
industrial business sales rose 13%.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Earnings per share reached
$0.39.&#160; On a comparable basis, excluding
restructuring charges, earnings per share increased 11% to $0.41.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SPARKS, MD, MARCH&nbsp;27
- - - - McCormick&nbsp;&amp; Company, Incorporated (NYSE:MKC), today reported
record results for the first quarter ended February&nbsp;29, 2008.&#160; Earnings per share were $0.39 compared to
$0.33 in the first quarter of 2007.&#160; On a
comparable basis with 2007, excluding restructuring charges, the Company
increased earnings per share 11% to $0.41.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Alan D. Wilson, President
and CEO, commented, &#147;We are off to a good start in fiscal year 2008 with a
strong first quarter.&#160; Higher pricing and
volume and the benefit of favorable foreign exchange rates drove an 11% sales
increase.&#160; Each segment and region of the
business grew sales during this period.&#160;
With these first quarter results, the addition of Billy Bee Honey
Products and our outlook for the next three quarters, we are increasing our
2008 sales growth outlook to 5 to 7% from 4 to 6%.&#160; This range excludes sales related to the
pending acquisition of the Lawry&#146;s business.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Margins remain under
pressure from higher and more volatile commodity costs.&#160; However, we have taken pricing actions early
in the year and expect to continue to see the benefit from these actions in
future quarters.&#160; Cost savings from our
restructuring plan and supply chain initiatives are providing an additional
offset to higher costs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are reaffirming this
year&#146;s goal to achieve earnings per share of $1.97 to $2.01 which includes an
estimated $0.10 of restructuring charges.&#160;
On a comparable basis with 2007, excluding restructuring charges, this
is an increase of 8 to 10%.&#160; Our business
strategy and performance are delivering great results and providing fuel for
investments in brand marketing and other growth initiatives.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales in the first
quarter rose 11%, including the impact of foreign exchange rates which added
4%.&#160; Higher pricing, volume increases in
branded spices and seasonings, and new products contributed to this increase<i>.</i>&#160; Operating income
rose 17%, which was an increase of 10% excluding restructuring charges.&#160; The Company was able to offset a steep
increase in commodity costs with pricing actions.&#160; Operating income also benefited from cost
savings related to the restructuring program and additional expense reductions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\cball\08-9028-1\task2811449\9028-1-ma.htm',USER='cball',CD='Mar 26 18:20 2008' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings
per share were $0.39 compared to $0.33 in the first quarter of 2007.&#160; Charges related to the Company&#146;s
restructuring program reduced earnings per share $0.02 in the first quarter of
2008 compared to a reduction of $0.04 in the first quarter of 2007.&#160; Excluding the impact of restructuring
charges, earnings per share rose $0.04, an 11% increase over the first quarter
of 2007.&#160; Higher operating income added
$0.04 per share, lower shares outstanding added $0.01 per share and a reduction
in income from unconsolidated operations decreased earnings per share by $0.01
during the first quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cash
from operations was $24 million compared to negative cash from operations in
the first quarter of 2007.&#160; This improved
result was largely due to receivables collections, the timing of tax payments,
lower retirement plan contributions and a decrease in payments related to the
restructuring plan.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Business
Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Consumer
Business</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">66,977</font></b></p>

  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:1.44%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; For the first quarter, sales for McCormick&#146;s consumer
business rose 10% and 5% in local currency.&#160;
This increase was driven by higher volume as well as pricing
actions.&#160;&#160; Consumer sales in the Americas
rose 8% due to increased volume from revitalization activity, ethnic products
and new items, as well as higher prices.&#160;
Foreign exchange rates added 1% to sales in this region.&#160; Consumer sales in Europe increased 12% and 3%
in local currency.&#160; This increase was
driven by higher prices as well as incremental sales from the Thai Kitchen
acquisition, increased marketing support and merchandising improvements<i>. </i>&#160;&#160;In the
Asia/Pacific region, sales rose 14% and 3% in local currency, led by gains in
China.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the first quarter,
consumer business operating income excluding restructuring charges rose to
$67.0 million from $60.2 million in 2007, an increase of 11%.&#160; This increase was due to higher sales and
improved operating income margin.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the first quarter,
sales for McCormick&#146;s industrial business increased 13% and 10% in local
currency.&#160; Pricing has been and continues
to be increased to reflect higher costs of flour, soy oil, cheese and other
commodities.&#160; A favorable product mix </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">also added to first
quarter sales.&#160; Industrial sales in the
Americas rose 10% and 8% in local currency with increased sales to both food
manufacturers and food service customers<i>. </i>&#160;In Europe, sales rose 17% and 12% in local
currency with continued increases in seasonings for poultry and for snack
products.&#160; Sales in the Asia/Pacific
region rose 24% and 13% in local currency with increases to the restaurant
industry as well as other food manufacturers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the first quarter,
industrial business operating income excluding restructuring charges rose to
$14.3 million from $14.0 million in 2007, an increase of 2%.&#160; The gain from higher sales was offset in part
by continued increases and volatility in the cost of certain commodities.&#160; The Company has made and continues to make
progress in working with its strategic customers to contract for future
purchases and pass through higher costs with increased prices.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP
Financial Measures</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The pro forma information
excluding restructuring charges in this press release are not measures that are
defined in generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;).&#160; Management believes the pro forma information
is important for purposes of comparison to prior periods and development of
future projections and earnings growth prospects.&#160;&#160; This information is also used by management
to measure the profitability of our on-going operations.&#160; Management analyzes the Company&#146;s business
performance and trends excluding amounts related to the restructuring.&#160; These measures provide a more consistent view
of performance than the closest GAAP equivalent for management and
investors.&#160; Management compensates for
this by using these measures in combination with the GAAP measures.&#160; The presentation of the non-GAAP measures in
this press release are made alongside the most directly comparable GAAP
measures.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pro
forma Information</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company has provided
below certain pro forma financial results excluding amounts related to a
restructuring program in 2008 and 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">McCormick&nbsp;&amp;
Company, Incorporated is the global leader in the manufacture, marketing and
distribution of spices, seasonings and flavors to the entire food industry &#151; to
foodservice and food manufacturers as well as to retail outlets.</font></p>
